# Creating ELK Stack v8.17.2 with Cowrie honeypot



## ELK Stack Setup
**Created by: Azrin Putra**
**Created: 12/11/2024**










#### **1. Preparing Ubuntu Server**
1.  Download latest Ubuntu server from Ubuntu official site
- Ubuntu official site
[https://ubuntu.com/download/server#instant-vms](https://ubuntu.com/download/server#instant-vms)

2. Install Ubuntu iso on Vmware
- Install steps (Click next unless specified below)
	1. Select create a new virtual machine

3. Configuring Ubuntu for LAN network use behind my PFsense firewall
- Configuration
	1. After booting up, run `sudo apt update && upgrade`
	2. Since we will be putting ELK in LAN, let’s setup the networking for ELK
	- ELK LAN setup
		1. Run cd `/etc/netplan` to find our config file `00-installer-config.yaml`. If it doesn’t exist, create one and nano into it
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/ac38a617-9b0f-4c67-b410-e0ff960058f4/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466YDF6H4E6%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090058Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIFQuHz8THaRyxbxFxp2WjnhtZun6vM6GjCq3858vgyDcAiEAsTozowD9a7sLFXpblAC73jqmi7wXwksIqohs8OmmEGUq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDEd10%2Ff%2BsDrNCNHWyircAw%2B5Gi2xplqfRgZtR09eAX%2FG%2FTz96zKTssQ2ngKyy5mSzWQg%2BCpw0dWwRGrQTmVDDTO%2Bx0QrYhUKymw3n8iQSxfzd8dlT3c79fH8l0NnUcLB2ElldMq8NylpTEVXrIBzuJjEL4xVF5%2BNCjZnldIYmJnq0vsIMrgiGu6DGhsq%2F%2BRgmLuNQoEoYjw%2FYDtdiKfp0LGjbz2jUVS0lv5a3p1uPa8X3D2xZzR%2FJ8G5OFCHFcx3CerNqP2T2yh0fKeMs%2FmeUDMDJyZR0Il7n7EsyruIOZa8gGPEMPcohexedJPAr7D4pr5H2FqyVtdkPhN1i8d5tSLlyO%2FGAjGcpSb%2FILZPPzDPGMgiXZvRSC1YBZpouhN9hXX1VaEJW6BJicBdwS8PrrQHeD5dZZAOVp61pjf4Ks4qqihGbMzbz4QPSz9CIH7i1Q8CCWIyUMwzw0qR5w2DmQTk1cisAe01LnD3eI8cJSkmf64wyrZYU5sFrGOTRIKTFbWRtrRW33JapdkaDq8UovWNb0golnbL%2FT4oPji7liPYy3HMEiLc9%2FXJxz7bff%2F3QGcqSiD0%2FAX4vE3lePyBwl5JW%2BHs1h03QJX%2BTUzb41P5u8i6gQ6XMUbMdfBcyi4ZtEb2W%2FvWtdhXCrdjMICJ%2Fs0GOqUBv%2FdfiFPmW%2B0JV2R0xYViGVV3SaGAvwfTuo4A5BctaXOmSgSPh4SiMp3zSN5mFq8GunzcZS8ggUliXpl2kCecAHXkIxytLS0BP8MZqaQwK1r2i14%2FrpJG0m5WNzbTGCQjvBtDMz4FOaEmjEP0%2Fk0mRnbdRdcwpV%2By940Hpb%2F%2FyAS6f8HaLqTohe8u1kVAIL6Tvi8pLMRLUNifcw1GXiyi4JKMa488&X-Amz-Signature=8ccc39c04cce01ef2f4ada2613588f87dc3702178aeffffc7418b0834c0d9794&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

		2. Copy this configuration in the file and save it. Take note of the indentation. We are using IP <172.16.50.1> as that is our default gateway for our LAN network
```shell
network:
 version: 2
 renderer: networkd
 ethernets:
   ens33:
     dhcp4: no
     addresses:
       - 172.16.50.20/24
     routes:
     - to: default
       via: 172.16.50.1
     nameservers:
         addresses: [172.16.50.1]              
```

		3. Run `sudo netplan try` . Run `ip a` and `ping` 8.8.8.8 to test connection to the Web.

#### **2. Installing ELK**
- Installing Elasticsearch
	1. Install Elasticsearch from these  commands from [https://www.elastic.co/guide/en/elasticsearch/reference/8.15/deb.html#deb-repo](https://www.elastic.co/guide/en/elasticsearch/reference/8.15/deb.html#deb-repo)
```shell
wget -qO - https://artifacts.elastic.co/GPG-KEY-elasticsearch | sudo gpg --dearmor -o /usr/share/keyrings/elasticsearch-keyring.gpg
#Installing the public signing key

sudo apt-get install apt-transport-https
#Installing the apt-transport-https

echo "deb [signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/elasticsearch-keyring.gpg] https://artifacts.elastic.co/packages/8.x/apt stable main" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/elastic-8.x.list
#Saving repo definition in /etc/apt/sources.list.d/elastic-8.x.list

sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install elasticsearch
#Downloading and installing elasticsearch
```

	3. Run Elasticsearch
```shell
#Configure elasticsearch to run at boot
sudo apt-get update
sudo /bin/systemctl enable elasticsearch.service

#start/stop elasticsearch as a service
sudo systemctl start elasticsearch.service
sudo systemctl stop elasticsearch.servi
```

	4. Enable logging in systemd journal for Elasticsearch. Access the elasticsearch.service file via 
`sudo nano /lib/systemd/system/elasticsearch.service` and remove `—quiet` flag at Execstart=….
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/3580248d-526a-450c-bf0f-285c18433e83/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RTVEAECE%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIE3d5J8NHxrn9K5fhMskUN5LKx5zAEHzpGNHTvgKMxQEAiABTWcWc74lvkp64K5hR8hutZ01L6Ve80kfOHH1PZV%2FzSr%2FAwhfEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIML53N0fyoAkCW1xc%2BKtwDoI6wHxaVHPBqDyMj%2BmDk%2BWPrMOlCsNcNtGRnCwe8r8ng9uqDKak13RO9TI4eKLDhYuMD9nokH%2F0bImm2X1zTplsuf3pI2ic0TMbnO7z%2F9E4JJ%2B%2FZNzSIniZWHIqE%2BMXTCb1Tzn%2BwfZrj8Il4zHruGHHY4uTC%2BRmtVWHCHeB630bYjSIRtKp8Ou9ZmFwZp3lvG%2FVtsQgVfaZcWgR8e%2FC%2Fb4WiEI5sZJZ0mTDK69i5D5%2Bx%2BBryxBfTgB0Rq0hcPT0umiDzxWBoEKdbtMJ28Ewe0ydWTlzlJE3WmuN0sJDi2t10HgkK2%2Fv97L3W1sl3TfwuZZdznEYkmbclY5UZ5dNu3W7r21qzZq2zfIH2s3wZZNPlwrbY4jiiY3apN2G5Yd%2Fu3FaV3BcMdi0BI0YZ%2BElJwBENIlfMmB3fNNp9zK6vLocIxrXPoaraRCBkeipcD1cRIPVQ%2FUpL3iqAaaWdjYk95CRRCCK7%2Fd2kWSTJExHPRAbIo15%2FLi%2BG1So3ePeNyZACb8n76MUAQg%2F%2B%2BPLKR%2BX3%2FtCnd%2FB0e7NtDwjMEeNA5qCFM%2Fdm58hTjOX%2FiRlHTjxwAF1GSArVupRaIoIzb2UdxtqqWxqel4bVR6DSiAGNtgd6SG0ePlWPmMG4XTAw9Ij%2BzQY6pgHyJPajGwjCy3v3hJ2QPBDhnC9codMDRO7ZxQpZVZ4yibUHZxb6qhxDmCealjhrXW%2Fb7vBq97N3T08lNZLEEFpA1y9iPj8bwTqU8XsWfrh4YLlW68pq0RskLJMkTtY52AAc5%2BWk3DqdJsfBjKguE8IayJ%2Fk4mi3bI1WpGasMHilRPqE1pR%2B%2FK72%2Fr4i%2B2x4QX64YTfv6g1ciH51Rm6KNL%2BpF6OC%2BVz9&X-Amz-Signature=aa21ebd48a79181745bd3d88d5094e2db446de9b7693fb8a46b4df5a442a2c8f&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)
💡 After starting service, an error might occur as shown below which is seen via `systemctl status elasticsearch.service` .
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/3ae566ac-ade7-499d-99ce-082056a91183/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466TLKQ2KUJ%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090058Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCICXHwvlDuGpUl2e1aOkY1Ju%2Fuoh1cSEMNaq%2FZ8umcOGcAiEAy8kk6erTF42isxxjjxtMnbiIb2vCytN4pWgvieJ9Jqwq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDHTV6CiFYJWzv9A1oyrcA%2Fl47nBktCZgd5rYASf9UHrFt0FKB3q7f%2FyLLUzBa8Xh2Tt4YG81IBWewhmaTxCORxHSkRmo3mORRzX8XN5mRRnYAexhqaOUY6FniQLIfdOYzZN8Pa%2B7703Dlni5DSL5YkANnnjS1TpVcy8AeMsbFL2ks%2Bn1%2B4sxTFrPsD1yM%2F8EkjADPuA5kbrmZiWnR%2FHZtmT%2Bs96c%2BOs7S7ZIbwaJaMaaJu%2Fp%2FFDLpnNTB1Zp3JC6N1NV7MtRwZp%2BKzXnCluzJk7pwuSCUMIfjbcGlnI8m0lVZ5tmQZTPwUOnhBVwoxP9GIgl1A%2BtTYXtwb%2F7202REQYAebSD5RTCsqxTxn2gEJzPU7395YWEvIadLJjXSUUMRhl9IAY%2FTOmu5SJY8KxgbfqTvrd%2F8tEH5Pm3y%2BGXHvL7uj0TqyF%2BLoCR7Notqts9m9bbcvSE7rBr4krSXrycarZdLhHo5kwXQMqSyIVzxtwY5LF6TcP%2FyfV1ArfFs8aMkJpT4s1PFaLJOU3FVEEvM9oPHUTzY0z93Ro%2FyE4ySsBN%2FjzoeoKOM8G0%2BddJL8BHnvliJvtTMqIT9IGzkfNJKGecDrNPQBO0ZKFSzGu3jNKYeLlyRNT%2FX4MFMWn7%2FHlwbi1QyWCdE3zPCJwNMLmI%2Fs0GOqUBa2h%2FxKUG2siyOYYgP0ih3AbeyKGCcmPGat6zvrEQNjEJ7%2BQCNT%2FMJJGKXXFYn79nMqBrGqVuNk1XeaLqoUnR5kQtQsruEEkLj23wIa2hhARJd898t1Cz5coPAEE5oTH9aXfFKalyVsNmzsvLPoniezDgrBQ%2FQbETaMRYIsZNc%2FOQ9IlV1SmItkyZtsLfV2N0BBNg87q8b6unoukxOksWuKUTG9yq&X-Amz-Signature=3c898d062bfae8c53c6ff1a26a82def319d4d5e6ef7cf1ac3f4a6d3b1b708192&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)
It is just a formatting error in the elasticsearch.service. It can be fixed via formatting the [Unit] section as shown below.
[Unit]
Description=Elasticsearch
Documentation=https://www.elastic.co
Wants=network-online.target
After=network-online.target

	5. For Elasticsearch debugging via journalctl
```shell
#Tail journal to view in real time
sudo journalctl -f

#List only elasticsearch entries
sudo journalctl --unit elasticsearch

#Show entries at a specific time example
sudo journalctl --unit elasticsearch --since  "2016-10-30 18:17:16"
```

	6. Successful install and start

💡 Sometimes elasticsearch won’t start out of the box as a single node cluster so we need to tweak it in `/etc/elasticsearch/elasticsearch.yml `

We can change both names to the same value in this case, we will go with elkserver.

Once done, we can run `sudo systemctl daemon-reload` and `sudo service elasticsearch restart`. If successful, it will be shown like the example below.
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/25cea82a-cb12-4e38-a690-c2aa4f486bdb/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RTVEAECE%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIE3d5J8NHxrn9K5fhMskUN5LKx5zAEHzpGNHTvgKMxQEAiABTWcWc74lvkp64K5hR8hutZ01L6Ve80kfOHH1PZV%2FzSr%2FAwhfEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIML53N0fyoAkCW1xc%2BKtwDoI6wHxaVHPBqDyMj%2BmDk%2BWPrMOlCsNcNtGRnCwe8r8ng9uqDKak13RO9TI4eKLDhYuMD9nokH%2F0bImm2X1zTplsuf3pI2ic0TMbnO7z%2F9E4JJ%2B%2FZNzSIniZWHIqE%2BMXTCb1Tzn%2BwfZrj8Il4zHruGHHY4uTC%2BRmtVWHCHeB630bYjSIRtKp8Ou9ZmFwZp3lvG%2FVtsQgVfaZcWgR8e%2FC%2Fb4WiEI5sZJZ0mTDK69i5D5%2Bx%2BBryxBfTgB0Rq0hcPT0umiDzxWBoEKdbtMJ28Ewe0ydWTlzlJE3WmuN0sJDi2t10HgkK2%2Fv97L3W1sl3TfwuZZdznEYkmbclY5UZ5dNu3W7r21qzZq2zfIH2s3wZZNPlwrbY4jiiY3apN2G5Yd%2Fu3FaV3BcMdi0BI0YZ%2BElJwBENIlfMmB3fNNp9zK6vLocIxrXPoaraRCBkeipcD1cRIPVQ%2FUpL3iqAaaWdjYk95CRRCCK7%2Fd2kWSTJExHPRAbIo15%2FLi%2BG1So3ePeNyZACb8n76MUAQg%2F%2B%2BPLKR%2BX3%2FtCnd%2FB0e7NtDwjMEeNA5qCFM%2Fdm58hTjOX%2FiRlHTjxwAF1GSArVupRaIoIzb2UdxtqqWxqel4bVR6DSiAGNtgd6SG0ePlWPmMG4XTAw9Ij%2BzQY6pgHyJPajGwjCy3v3hJ2QPBDhnC9codMDRO7ZxQpZVZ4yibUHZxb6qhxDmCealjhrXW%2Fb7vBq97N3T08lNZLEEFpA1y9iPj8bwTqU8XsWfrh4YLlW68pq0RskLJMkTtY52AAc5%2BWk3DqdJsfBjKguE8IayJ%2Fk4mi3bI1WpGasMHilRPqE1pR%2B%2FK72%2Fr4i%2B2x4QX64YTfv6g1ciH51Rm6KNL%2BpF6OC%2BVz9&X-Amz-Signature=efe57c28beb84c621585d5dbda3f06aa7ad4dcaf35bffb70786662c788c7ba77&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

	7. We can check on the credentials and access to node via `curl -k --cacert /etc/elasticsearch/certs/http_ca.crt -u elastic:<elasticpassword> https://localhost:9200`
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/6ec0379f-aa63-4b07-939b-e2c7a4f50bf4/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RTVEAECE%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIE3d5J8NHxrn9K5fhMskUN5LKx5zAEHzpGNHTvgKMxQEAiABTWcWc74lvkp64K5hR8hutZ01L6Ve80kfOHH1PZV%2FzSr%2FAwhfEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIML53N0fyoAkCW1xc%2BKtwDoI6wHxaVHPBqDyMj%2BmDk%2BWPrMOlCsNcNtGRnCwe8r8ng9uqDKak13RO9TI4eKLDhYuMD9nokH%2F0bImm2X1zTplsuf3pI2ic0TMbnO7z%2F9E4JJ%2B%2FZNzSIniZWHIqE%2BMXTCb1Tzn%2BwfZrj8Il4zHruGHHY4uTC%2BRmtVWHCHeB630bYjSIRtKp8Ou9ZmFwZp3lvG%2FVtsQgVfaZcWgR8e%2FC%2Fb4WiEI5sZJZ0mTDK69i5D5%2Bx%2BBryxBfTgB0Rq0hcPT0umiDzxWBoEKdbtMJ28Ewe0ydWTlzlJE3WmuN0sJDi2t10HgkK2%2Fv97L3W1sl3TfwuZZdznEYkmbclY5UZ5dNu3W7r21qzZq2zfIH2s3wZZNPlwrbY4jiiY3apN2G5Yd%2Fu3FaV3BcMdi0BI0YZ%2BElJwBENIlfMmB3fNNp9zK6vLocIxrXPoaraRCBkeipcD1cRIPVQ%2FUpL3iqAaaWdjYk95CRRCCK7%2Fd2kWSTJExHPRAbIo15%2FLi%2BG1So3ePeNyZACb8n76MUAQg%2F%2B%2BPLKR%2BX3%2FtCnd%2FB0e7NtDwjMEeNA5qCFM%2Fdm58hTjOX%2FiRlHTjxwAF1GSArVupRaIoIzb2UdxtqqWxqel4bVR6DSiAGNtgd6SG0ePlWPmMG4XTAw9Ij%2BzQY6pgHyJPajGwjCy3v3hJ2QPBDhnC9codMDRO7ZxQpZVZ4yibUHZxb6qhxDmCealjhrXW%2Fb7vBq97N3T08lNZLEEFpA1y9iPj8bwTqU8XsWfrh4YLlW68pq0RskLJMkTtY52AAc5%2BWk3DqdJsfBjKguE8IayJ%2Fk4mi3bI1WpGasMHilRPqE1pR%2B%2FK72%2Fr4i%2B2x4QX64YTfv6g1ciH51Rm6KNL%2BpF6OC%2BVz9&X-Amz-Signature=a9e5a3a6e40417048e56d264e5bdab0390c05e99e202d95c1519695b3a891c23&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

💡 If errors occur, most likely it is a credential issue. We can check the password or just reset it via `/usr/share/elasticsearch/bin/elasticsearch-reset-password -u elastic -i -v` and just follow the steps.

- Installing Kibana
	1. Run `sudo apt-get update` && `sudo apt-get install kibana` 
 [https://www.elastic.co/guide/en/kibana/8.15/deb.html#deb-repo](https://www.elastic.co/guide/en/kibana/8.15/deb.html#deb-repo)

	2. Open /etc/kibana/kibana.yml and adjust the following. Make sure to run `sudo systemctl daemon-reload` , `systemctl enable kibana` & `sudo service kibana start` once done.
```shell
#Set server.host
server.host: "0.0.0.0"


```

	3. Save and restart Kibana service. Now if we go to the web browser with our <elkserver ip> through port 5601, we should get to Elastic’s setup page.
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/7bba5cfd-1395-47f8-b9ad-6f155e014f35/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466Y2VFBF5S%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCIFgzfK9H5K%2BG5AvOF1feyitoA2eiwBmNmZEaaf%2FQxCfAAiAxl2c5ropr%2FVNEeNf1mDsfIZH5PDDlWrs6VSaQ2oWWVyr%2FAwhfEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMDcwDtzC8iWYvwj3dKtwDXuv8AYdnO7NXKQZAbFTugigBn0K%2B18wR0%2B9K%2BqrEscF48LpkWaCQB2y0Qal39AQy6vDypX5l7n0olwRXzUQJLGTX7R02pS0Hg92MTPSAsFrkpj3%2B9%2FvK5Y5IiEiEOsZNpfWk5RXMVWWBxEXp7YaTJazBW8xusDzMstldPCKHP4vhYj%2FM5P9XAhwyLgJAeDHT%2BCe0BtRXRbBCxihW%2B1uXH6XPc8oIepORwrRAp%2FRrPmiY%2FA6UkVrRozuL66wN%2BrKT73usdQ4uCtEnvVPE8NVoq4ISycC8RqAjsa44lHLbJxxQa9SKowSEBBBjqh0EPzSSi5zkj13iW7PoRGun%2BAEKqYXLBaK34ysoEI5azdam4iVqBW4ZheaxERakefVh%2BB9HydorT63YRaDdFdnhF6zWSTZ31L1JL9ztnwkBhAuns3FLlJZKy4WRe98seMzqDE7ACgAK8oDMyisjQQX2lSd6ek9eHRbWfxnzngBKTHBxd8LqrPerC38AvQujtj0F6aC1gx7L1lb1qJhHueJEifmwEpUV6OdExDU7dWWCFP6lCjI%2Fz9xbBaFBm2oA%2FRSGT7eKt8FTbB%2FerHakMl3UldRX1CXiVy1X746vTdqelDPpzYxeqYzGqsAjIq4BqQwwooj%2BzQY6pgEOyaiHZF1uzYeIfX%2BoFrB4awGCfjZkv48i06ky5j6SAYIu1rgCsZq5IwmakVT8VuS5G%2FN1E%2F7tc173azd0d77jf3qnIOxyAqsfyFLcHifLVH3BDtjf5H7oZSsYvtYYhxiK1gL4ZYM5DVN9SSr9p8EzuoiGM87tL6W1YsnZiAXii%2F4scL7TlUnd8v1n4xxkr77tz1bBM3%2BW%2FasxkvQYmhQegzw09etj&X-Amz-Signature=a608caeba7795d16f6355dec33ed21589ed2f67b353870d86e777fdb919cd255&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

💡 If there is a active firewall, make sure to allow traffic to port 5601.

	4. Click on Where do i find this and run the command given on elkserver

We will need to add the full path and sudo which would look like this:
`sudo /usr/share/elasticsearch/bin/elasticsearch-create-enrollment-token --scope kibana`
and we will get a long string in reply

	5. Enter the enrollment token in the text box and click Configure Elastic

	6. Get the verification code by running `sudo /usr/share/kibana/bin/kibana-verification-code` and enter it in the pop up window

- Installing Logstash
	1. Run `sudo apt update && sudo apt install logstash`
[https://www.elastic.co/downloads/logstash](https://www.elastic.co/downloads/logstash)

	2. Run `sudo systemctl daemon-reload && systemctl enable logstash`
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/26b8227a-a6f9-40a7-8d76-248b9a7826f0/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB46665RDE2JC%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIDpqvhJIhkfNF%2BLtjCYloQ4z02dDN5Nf0OjnIM5qkm3YAiEA%2FaUVe%2FkuYlFpVk1WZyeI1nHoqtvM0EaL%2F3h2emIcwycq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDHDa7JYOlURDaTowESrcA%2ByUVKHmrfGyO70PMR%2B5KDcsS4PtqV9%2F3wWgONg1B9r1GjYn%2BSNI8qMPrAD24ORA733Ph4YDbBoFzA9ouADGCJqet8LnV1NJ8mCeAfovDQVHyVzytktD%2FIBVFq0U30g3QTlhl8a9pSbDY%2B460jO8Mb%2FWSwepxbiVwPMXnw%2B30R%2Bu9IX6hIM83XTQIG39xPfn6%2F9ARdtLH%2FruyKfxE8R7VoObzWM%2Ftfxvuw8En33M%2BVoeK%2FA%2F%2BTq7IpLeBkF9QYV1AjWjBZYvHZJBhco2V1i8k49Ph5hJoOw887lUP5zttJLzyFdZ1mv597ON6XS0vaQ2wJL4uWQzFIay%2BAginrmoEwkRncWQ6qv8uFArD9LOqeSKr%2FUlmDoP%2F8S4DvZ7Cx5OxSShNaar06Wk6%2Fq9QtE2724a5Im5yT4augHLCY4myo2osM%2BxjwETqV0NV5cRMkz5NUoU%2F24v5I38A%2BbOfqLkeWpufCb2FZmBBw6fSpusUjj4%2Bebjz%2B5Ysf9v1DndxQkeXpzCFezpQ8xD3%2B71JrbgsNkUFiGuEyWDDGRy%2BgVyunrWi6tvPP9Zv0KmY3bZotO8BGwS3qu8V7wnzHwgYhdp9TOAN2jqCApAInnOiDO3Dy3X9wcdR1lVBsn7CdgcMPeI%2Fs0GOqUBFrVXohzu1K2TYsLjyIjwD2khXbq1GRXBWs%2BFj3RLA8Lon23F5eLMU6DvuFSsh%2BjcO87Wo9n%2FITohF005NsFWo6883EcMll5etpM4qW7WNwtl8KaRsK9H%2Bl%2Fdt6wuT7nAvrukzTWc94vkoY%2FkLkYXDkSifFLC3k8kN7uRorSvpx%2BbYfnMfHDfJY8QSq%2BtBbdxweNrTdDDnjE5e4xCTe0v4Po7ngJQ&X-Amz-Signature=ba30da446d52d1e34a6d12d654995cdbee50fc27dcd44ae1dc3416a537b2a07a&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

	3. Open /etc/logstash and access the conf.d directory so that we can tweak our config file. 
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/7c12758d-494a-4459-b92f-4b2485498e62/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB46665RDE2JC%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIDpqvhJIhkfNF%2BLtjCYloQ4z02dDN5Nf0OjnIM5qkm3YAiEA%2FaUVe%2FkuYlFpVk1WZyeI1nHoqtvM0EaL%2F3h2emIcwycq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDHDa7JYOlURDaTowESrcA%2ByUVKHmrfGyO70PMR%2B5KDcsS4PtqV9%2F3wWgONg1B9r1GjYn%2BSNI8qMPrAD24ORA733Ph4YDbBoFzA9ouADGCJqet8LnV1NJ8mCeAfovDQVHyVzytktD%2FIBVFq0U30g3QTlhl8a9pSbDY%2B460jO8Mb%2FWSwepxbiVwPMXnw%2B30R%2Bu9IX6hIM83XTQIG39xPfn6%2F9ARdtLH%2FruyKfxE8R7VoObzWM%2Ftfxvuw8En33M%2BVoeK%2FA%2F%2BTq7IpLeBkF9QYV1AjWjBZYvHZJBhco2V1i8k49Ph5hJoOw887lUP5zttJLzyFdZ1mv597ON6XS0vaQ2wJL4uWQzFIay%2BAginrmoEwkRncWQ6qv8uFArD9LOqeSKr%2FUlmDoP%2F8S4DvZ7Cx5OxSShNaar06Wk6%2Fq9QtE2724a5Im5yT4augHLCY4myo2osM%2BxjwETqV0NV5cRMkz5NUoU%2F24v5I38A%2BbOfqLkeWpufCb2FZmBBw6fSpusUjj4%2Bebjz%2B5Ysf9v1DndxQkeXpzCFezpQ8xD3%2B71JrbgsNkUFiGuEyWDDGRy%2BgVyunrWi6tvPP9Zv0KmY3bZotO8BGwS3qu8V7wnzHwgYhdp9TOAN2jqCApAInnOiDO3Dy3X9wcdR1lVBsn7CdgcMPeI%2Fs0GOqUBFrVXohzu1K2TYsLjyIjwD2khXbq1GRXBWs%2BFj3RLA8Lon23F5eLMU6DvuFSsh%2BjcO87Wo9n%2FITohF005NsFWo6883EcMll5etpM4qW7WNwtl8KaRsK9H%2Bl%2Fdt6wuT7nAvrukzTWc94vkoY%2FkLkYXDkSifFLC3k8kN7uRorSvpx%2BbYfnMfHDfJY8QSq%2BtBbdxweNrTdDDnjE5e4xCTe0v4Po7ngJQ&X-Amz-Signature=ef55f9f51462bc2ece17a71f0c2af9013520430088b9d93589f0d0cebd68db98&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

Since there is nothing inside the directory, we need to copy the `logstash-sample.conf` file into this directory and do our configuration.
`sudo cp /etc/logstash/logstash-sample.conf .`

	4. Open the file and change the hosts to our <elkserver ip> and the password to <elasticpassword>
Default

This is caused by the self signed ssl key. We need to go back to the logstash-sample.conf file that we edited and add these lines `ssl_verification_mode ⇒ "none"` & `ssl_enabled ⇒ false` to turn off ssl certificate verification.
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/df7b1d68-b723-4859-b3d4-c79153d0b676/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB46665RDE2JC%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIDpqvhJIhkfNF%2BLtjCYloQ4z02dDN5Nf0OjnIM5qkm3YAiEA%2FaUVe%2FkuYlFpVk1WZyeI1nHoqtvM0EaL%2F3h2emIcwycq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDHDa7JYOlURDaTowESrcA%2ByUVKHmrfGyO70PMR%2B5KDcsS4PtqV9%2F3wWgONg1B9r1GjYn%2BSNI8qMPrAD24ORA733Ph4YDbBoFzA9ouADGCJqet8LnV1NJ8mCeAfovDQVHyVzytktD%2FIBVFq0U30g3QTlhl8a9pSbDY%2B460jO8Mb%2FWSwepxbiVwPMXnw%2B30R%2Bu9IX6hIM83XTQIG39xPfn6%2F9ARdtLH%2FruyKfxE8R7VoObzWM%2Ftfxvuw8En33M%2BVoeK%2FA%2F%2BTq7IpLeBkF9QYV1AjWjBZYvHZJBhco2V1i8k49Ph5hJoOw887lUP5zttJLzyFdZ1mv597ON6XS0vaQ2wJL4uWQzFIay%2BAginrmoEwkRncWQ6qv8uFArD9LOqeSKr%2FUlmDoP%2F8S4DvZ7Cx5OxSShNaar06Wk6%2Fq9QtE2724a5Im5yT4augHLCY4myo2osM%2BxjwETqV0NV5cRMkz5NUoU%2F24v5I38A%2BbOfqLkeWpufCb2FZmBBw6fSpusUjj4%2Bebjz%2B5Ysf9v1DndxQkeXpzCFezpQ8xD3%2B71JrbgsNkUFiGuEyWDDGRy%2BgVyunrWi6tvPP9Zv0KmY3bZotO8BGwS3qu8V7wnzHwgYhdp9TOAN2jqCApAInnOiDO3Dy3X9wcdR1lVBsn7CdgcMPeI%2Fs0GOqUBFrVXohzu1K2TYsLjyIjwD2khXbq1GRXBWs%2BFj3RLA8Lon23F5eLMU6DvuFSsh%2BjcO87Wo9n%2FITohF005NsFWo6883EcMll5etpM4qW7WNwtl8KaRsK9H%2Bl%2Fdt6wuT7nAvrukzTWc94vkoY%2FkLkYXDkSifFLC3k8kN7uRorSvpx%2BbYfnMfHDfJY8QSq%2BtBbdxweNrTdDDnjE5e4xCTe0v4Po7ngJQ&X-Amz-Signature=f03e8481dec66c815e5d64f292afa26971aec7dee0dc03d2e292c22839d1fcdd&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)
```shell
output {
  elasticsearch {
    hosts => ["https://172.16.50.20:9200"]
    index => "%{[@metadata][beat]}-%{[@metadata][version]}-%{+YYYY.MM.dd}"
    user => "elastic"
    password => "Vd14k388sf7CxE4ahy8c"
    ssl_enabled => false
		ssl_verification_mode => "none"
  }
}

#We can run the code below to test config first before starting the service
sudo /usr/share/logstash/bin/logstash --path.settings /etc/logstash -t
```

💡 We need to find out more regarding this ssl certificate verification later.

	6. Once done, run `systemctl daemon-reload && sudo systemctl restart logstash`. If successful, we should see this below.

	1. Click on the burger on the top left hand corner and click on Fleet

	2. Click on Add Fleet Server

	3. Make sure that it is on Quick Start since we are using self signed certs and input your <elkserver IP:8220> into the input box together with server name. Click Continue.

💡 Ignore the ip addresses as it had went through a few reinstallations and just treat it as <YOURELKIPADDRESS>


	4. Under the Install Fleet Server to a centralized host, we can see all the commands that has been generated by Elastic and we can proceed to run all of it one at a time for debugging purposes
```shell
#all the configured commands from Elastic to my elkserver machine
sudo ./elastic-agent install \
  --fleet-server-es=https://172.16.50.20:9200 \
  --fleet-server-service-token=AAEAAWVsYXN0aWMvZmxlZXQtc2VydmVyL3Rva2VuLTE3MzE0NzIzODY2NzE6OEFiWDlMdjRTOUtBTzdLdWRkbHgtUQ \
  --fleet-server-policy=fleet-server-policy \
  --fleet-server-es-ca-trusted-fingerprint=689c68e24f3f09929fa9b2e587ec9cb2f9051c72d7fe1f4bb78b90fe9fa03fa5 \
  --fleet-server-port=8220
```

	5. If all commands are successful, we will see this in our elkserver

- Install Elastic Agent on a Windows machine(DC) to send logs to ELK stack 
	1. Click on Add agent
![image.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/98bb9fbc-f4b1-4e26-aff6-589ab646e8c1/image.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466YCR7UJLU%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIGXWJZ0AgQN%2B3k6lbuRuFepgVS0x5aoHn3zhCqaasDtoAiEAv5nEanRlR%2BAEWE1KPtfBIFx98%2FA9T80AcaQIBUPxvXwq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDA9%2BkBb5TDqWBr7dmSrcAxNj2xqp3NiPnHOz875eZ0KhRNqZiaREcRQKkf7mLlJ2eM99lelxdJlusIC2O%2FEIUFWyZ5QNyZs4Uv63oNxAOuP%2BMXprJgU0gYGI%2B0zwW4hEZ0bd%2FzDwpAKB0wHD5kwgrcCJ7imkudZYf6vf14I4SxuC19ORbhC3%2BCCQo%2BA8IlchhdxKHRkvWYbabSVgeY5Q6ProPsw0eAFSNjnuNcYVkD2fNIRa5PRRVaZD8f2qGW%2Fw7llFPEVUSwJ18V8b9lv7mYl4b5RKPd8EZR1IqArU%2FcUvySSGDqx3v0CJzFeQljmOIwLBAhUZx1vv9AmcVjCaSDAd1ALxn76SNZMZc59SrOWUyh07DaFLd%2BgLWy4pgU4hwmjhYaKYnWACvq6N%2FHVy%2FOz4I%2FpP7UOBZ1d3BScW0RcNdLuaRLsYt%2FJ56rCnHea5DgBIqfy1vXP7FD0JGj0V85fiqGYwGxoJ%2BaUWLMmxHrw2yCQUQr%2BOsqJ0Ajyjx07fQtxSDUyLl%2FNhRd%2BENhlYrsbxsHSJpGn%2BiNqbelcxuBFy3Lf4f9ilMDULfUU%2F8heNYOwCRRXq6YYuxPC5osHyC5aOnIIWYYSwEdl6%2B0hjIwFCUC5qyKhJSSquC0ieOYN7Us9BasCuOD%2BcNFujMLeJ%2Fs0GOqUB1W88HmzhsAXoOAiS5npLNy8zpIWnMCUNg6qSeyq0AUAzACnwf3xAT7DIZVFTyTfAuRghoGH2IhDeG0KQUfx9yMhSKSjUWo4BxdT7x1qQEhjJzOTGOB0NKLxL9DOS%2BJp%2Bgx5V1oql47ffXFQTxMPKr75%2FS9pgbHvI2QI9nowjKgR3f85Op1LV%2BWrQGSu%2FGKSJ1mY1qBWcbfqsUbpf%2BwT0pdrm88UW&X-Amz-Signature=51bb62e6d71458c83dc19698d25c973b78ef8ba81732f49d476495808c4084f3&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

	2. Name the agent policy as Windows, leave all as default and click create agent policy

	3. Make sure that the Enroll in Fleet option is selected

	4. Next let’s setup the windows elastic agent by scrolling down and clicking on the windows tab. Then we will just need to run the commands specified to install the elastic agent on our windows machine.

💡 Before running the last step which is .\elastic-agent.exe install, we need to edit the elastic-agent.yml file in the elastic-agent folder first to include our host ip and credentials. Here is an example below.

After saving the file, make sure to run the last command with an `—insecure` flag as we are using a self signed certificate

- Pfsense Integration 
	1. Search for pfSense in Integrations and click on pfSense

	2. Click on Add pfSense

	6. Under “Where to add this integration?”, select Fleet Server Policy under Existing Hosts

#### 4. Creating a HoneyPot on a Linux Server
- Installing Cowrie on the webserver
- Getting Logs from Cowrie and into ELK stack
	1. Add Elastic’s repository and key
```bash
$ wget -qO - https://artifacts.elastic.co/GPG-KEY-elasticsearch | sudo gpg --dearmor -o /usr/share/keyrings/elasticsearch-keyring.gpg
$ echo "deb https://artifacts.elastic.co/packages/8.x/apt stable main" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/elastic-8.x.list
$ apt-get update
```
	2. Install filebeat
```bash
$ sudo apt -y install apt-transport-https wget default-jre
$ sudo apt install filebeat
$ sudo apt install nginx apache2-utils
```
	3. Enable Filebeat
```bash
$ sudo systemctl enable filebeat
#Enable filebeat
```

If the installation is successful and filebeat is running, we should see this below

![Screenshot_2025-02-12_at_3.44.15_PM.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/6a6efd5e-2332-4ce4-ad5f-7f00a61fa49c/Screenshot_2025-02-12_at_3.44.15_PM.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RMGPY3XF%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIQDXzFZLPwKc%2FhnL8i7C%2FrGVdLakQTqf6iBjXf5OFtRIXAIgb1un46SWu%2FQoNvaJwbIknxUFeu0DTcnUvPN9Ong1cJwq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDIh2LNNVvZR%2FAfLV2yrcA9lDqwNBJkjgYz9LcLAbX8VayKeojlA61tEJvAUJn7E2ITEnqKe3rbSGSCRHYClfqFxvufMfNj8%2Bn1wqX8tGpLlXjkit9aeYOM7uhLf1FJZZSqphF0JepNMd6GhDrvWPqjdzhqdYjE2hgoRuFNUCtPCSs3JiGCy9OcHVBrHe2Ir8gCyvFFx9k2dIca0%2B8n8eusiXaNj8RBl%2F9XPtFnQI%2B4VmYASkaX9Ai%2BHD4RKdje7BPZV8p41Q%2FkQMh5pRiPZsEk5UL8%2FtOhjrc9GgLusYVHE7JRmYp5AXz3afqXZLe7bcxiahhuJ5EJYfi7CgGZihOl4YO6JwnGeztbATto%2FZLwjIfMsRlYE%2Bt4ywtJhJcxPYVqWRf%2FEwu1lwsHKKn3rs13t7LIy1228lqwQx7YgRi%2FJXkdHrdcS1ixvk%2FtXWjMxL0crVWI319UkAxvuDihM%2FfkjFV9gSwQr9FdvEAL4PZcm5ZKUTtV%2BPDkdbRajvkh6HCU48GLBc85F2kYujMjM2HQ4xyeW8Qol8QCIm7wxhI6FDuckQJZ9vexRRW76tdIPBQUAS5eUEcjfCW%2BFK3NyVvs7fH0pj%2F9dRPGt%2FPmveEDmdNyTy5rWtnFNrZ3Q%2FA0iw4WhNUgy9FgCsbX0FMJ2J%2Fs0GOqUBSOxG50yKqmG8jHK6QL%2BEcZ%2FPj7lNuzvA6lymXQgqVh7XMteCDPHFWZpORqU26XQ1%2FzQ%2F64Ay82NNu7t0fSdU1qBfYIERUc%2FYvXPuN2PjNw83NDYcwWT2VqrFQFwtpji%2BJA34OXGiICJRhhwBrSCxGvrbg5Pu%2BS3QbLnr1umv69Eqh9xRfFEU3TLgk7y%2FYvd8j08BsKFtek7nDmPFgZpqK0THfXd7&X-Amz-Signature=61c014b5d14f5d388910d5149da5f78caff43452931cf22ae7b3532fffa987fd&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

	4. Configuring Filebeat
We need to reconfigure the filebeat.yml file for Cowrie’s use
```bash
$ cd /etc/filebeat
```

Open the filebeat.yml file and do the following changes
		- Under filebeat inputs, change and add the following parameters 
```bash
# ============================== Filebeat inputs ===============================

filebeat.inputs:

# Each - is an input. Most options can be set at the input level, so
# you can use different inputs for various configurations.
# Below are the input-specific configurations.

# filestream is an input for collecting log messages from files.
- type: log

  # Unique ID among all inputs, an ID is required.
  #id: my-filestream-id

  # Change to true to enable this input configuration.
  enabled: true

  # Paths that should be crawled and fetched. Glob based paths.
  paths:
    - /home/cowrie/cowrie/var/log/cowrie/*.json
    #- c:\programdata\elasticsearch\logs\*

```
		- Comment all the Elasticsearch Output to prevent overlap
![Screenshot_2025-02-12_at_4.15.13_PM.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/1244f7d8-244f-4520-ade8-dfe69a857228/Screenshot_2025-02-12_at_4.15.13_PM.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466Q33RF2M5%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090101Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIAq0hv6a2G55%2FrRYIZcQWkDNS%2BGhEEGJ0%2Fmtm%2BGZP9S8AiEAlTjo%2FrDnvEhjRR%2FJQbCg%2FRd2h%2FD3CguYJkuGJ%2B0X8r0q%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDPc8W%2FGPFkHicCnHAyrcA11EMerd9Ce%2BE2%2FsH7mjqorg0xaApqLzL42HdahZPISzUs0YV5as6ZBlyUfrHv%2FghKmNd0wPs05xRFVUbNj4dJjBqKRzr5%2B0dqH0S1kOabxOz3t9nunThK8WIJq7abG6YrbkuWx88xqoHtnbPx%2F00MThfCqe3cwvK%2B2Fh0iErPSUHXUzEat%2FvYCAfgdsydGdKwe%2FsMe3e3wi9JByTquQMe9ol3wIj0RHxkusNxOPe92z3sBrx97MuWrCZygWkDXQo%2BvI9Mq8yZ3M9QakPVLdlo3tLAtcJm2smJ%2FGz7L5ns1hMiVLDMh8CToLnyvm67T2F%2FNCFGLhjd37%2BnNte2FIcKX3jXLU6ib7nJNxzzOHao9%2Bq20dsAYAnbfbD%2Bp8L%2F3HYCgVPKuofyCDSP1MG%2Fi3Ce3G6bF4qLVCPRCE5HOZsj9o6105CWmIisG4kcaMl%2BB19uBgXF7km8oanfxPigHRQEagli7l4HzPVIfqjf7GVKBV1KDGxlVYYEIl26FHqvMLhHfNl0TOwlg7RYhoZeBZuLyBsYRPNgQDRm3zgPOJ9vQEMcSFiC0M0Fc9%2B972jPji9C53dcryyvaXp8pVBA1jwJIDA5vYsmRjCvgNenCTAdr53Fyni4omKCgzMu%2B2MKuJ%2Fs0GOqUBE2WA3okFQOz%2F0r2n2Zxs%2FRUJGFspsuyynotThaowjXBdbdyixqYF1zf6AHa8v4yVtkHKMEoFo4ULBjiuRVnOwXcJtferFxgubD2rs0F9oSz8QnOdn5FoWRewGiMAbJ%2F0iM7MpJ%2BpjELJ1IySLgbeDKxJNa8RHwV917fhwtA%2BqYMUyOIYmir30okGbBZQJ8fyiGbbOUAF%2FGQcdA0KdBKbOy3JwYOD&X-Amz-Signature=233f271aeb478451fe71884a144844e06fe75aa1531fc56c648cf2803fa53d82&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

		- Uncomment output.logstash under Logstash Output and replace [localhost](http://localhost/) with your ELK IP address
```bash
# ------------------------------ Logstash Output -------------------------------
output.logstash:
  # The Logstash hosts
  hosts: ["172.16.66.100:5044"]
```

		- Run this command to check the filebeat config
```bash
$ sudo filebeat test config
$ sudo filebeat test output
```

	5. Go to the logstash folder on your ELK MACHINE and download the logstash-cowrie into the folder
```bash
$ cd /etc/logstash
$ curl -O https://github.com/cowrie/cowrie/blob/main/docs/elk/logstash-cowrie.conf
#This is the configuration file for Cowrie
```

	6. Open the downloaded logstash-cowrie file and change the following
		- Edit the output section at the end
```bash
output {
    if [type] == "cowrie" {
        elasticsearch {
            hosts => ["https://172.16.66.100:9200"]
            user => "elastic"
            password => "elastic"
            ssl => true
            cacert => "/etc/logstash/certs/http_ca.crt"
            ilm_enabled => auto
            ilm_rollover_alias => "cowrie-logstash"
        }
        #file {
        #    path => "/tmp/cowrie-logstash.log"
        #    codec => json
        #}
        stdout {
            codec => rubydebug
        }
    }
}

```

	7. Save the config file and run the following command to ensure that the configuration is ok
```bash
$ sudo /usr/share/logstash/bin/logstash --path.settings /etc/logstash/ -t -f /etc/logstash/conf.d/logstash-cowrie.conf
#If the configuration is correct, it should say configuration ok at the end

$ sudo journalctl -u logstash -f
#Check if there are any error in the logs
```

- Configuring ELK for proper parsing of Cowrie Logs
	1. We need to be able to separate Cowrie’s log from the other machines logs. We can do this by creating a data view for Cowrie.

	3. Click on Create data view

	4. We can then fill in the boxes

```plain text
#Name for our Cowrie Data View
1. Name - We will fill as Cowrie
#We need to make sure to select all the filebeat indexes with * as only Cowrie is using it 
2. Index Pattern - We will put "filebeat-*" 
3. Click Save Data View to Kibana
```

	5. Once done, we can then go back to the Discover tab and we should be able to see Cowrie under Data View
![seeCowrie.png](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/64e10e6c-af9d-4921-b1e8-2ada19725a23/dbeb3329-94d9-4dfe-a8ae-46546faf4e47/seeCowrie.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4664O6VQBOV%2F20260322%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260322T090057Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJb%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIQDh1tlUt9vtR%2Boh8xFYMkE2D8GrrJoKwQuEArmguHmH9AIgUGQ4cFZzTor%2F8f1ue1nMB1PubXcwO%2Bnu5v%2Foq6wx2Xwq%2FwMIXxAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDEOhwLy0SDsbSTLSGyrcA7CvniCjcLl%2BIN82mwQ2kf0zMrEYzul%2BDWooMg5pt3hQZnBrAH2IFEWFB9D9wSCi9QXWXoMWvH2G6DAfdVL3DADRMWIICSEzQiy2k2cjyCAHwL8fUfvuTVIV7bxLep1lW6Zph92yryXcb72KSZHxOO5UyDeD8C1lquNGYiPk9Ih6ICsI6h%2FgJGhUSxC%2FHK3sdSHPkkQTd%2FXr1BELNSDqXUUUYyRw4FRTK9Bbch6o1tXjiRBGeLVAXs1qnnRO%2Bc%2FItwIallvfsGg9PzO%2BlPaMN0QtH6IWze1Wthp4o%2FFBWQcCVzwyjWC6BAxHANgJZ2BuRwtZTlmpRbx3B1VVhHaQjqCLH3a%2FXZV9YqLKOf4UkMlYjXISbbPvgybaDheRO5om8PDXT4QTpNUKyTFCImCw0Vz3sY%2BIItz1OAqu8xRHCprQVI4%2BfGi73HE%2FcTP%2FupKTBJv%2F5XDXvTW4LV5fR7hsVYUNJi%2BprGVlz8gBkKWoEdSlm7tEjMfY90JNRBJD%2Fp5dS%2F494pAoPLWNl9zUP4y5p7LeYb0fYQRBZVJqa%2FvcrRFcl2ejAjU9Tym87QJctRwdP6f%2BCrwuLLPnZxepJOFqycu%2FryQccBZj2WB3baK7q6RVGHyVwm39rtiisQ5oMNyI%2Fs0GOqUBC7B0DkwBxY1gisbslNkkRj4eh7f%2FS%2FRHtLiZKBs9ul3qFml0cVFiwBXX97dCBguOMLsdSYBoBPs5OMQgvabovbQSYTlBUaj3tGklmVGl3%2F6aRyuTzO9ws2uKQOW94qNA5Q0tYC%2BhVz5f9kAmDyeN5sJj0OzYIh9H81qH4R9clcd1IMhVSaX%2F9UzlCm6oWXdBnvYszZbsK8g1qvb8XodDZz03GG7Z&X-Amz-Signature=933540bc74c5d92dc78137b83be9f6b734710617c0a6c8059c7ee1be351ebf0f&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

After clicking on Cowrie, we are able to see the full Cowrie logs. However some of the fields appear to be missing but appear in the JSON document.


	6. To enable more field detection, we need to add JSON parsing options in our `filebeat.yml`
```bash
  # Parse JSON logs properly
  json.keys_under_root: true
  json.add_error_key: true
  
  #After adding, restart filebeat
  
  $ sudo systemctl restart filebeat
```

After adding these lines in the filebeat.yml file, we can restart filebeat with systemctl and we should see more detailed fields appear under Discover in ELK 


#### 5. Creating Alerts on ELK to detect attacks on Cowrie
- Getting Started with custom alerts on ELK
	1. Under Observability, click on Alerts

	2. Click on Manage Rules

	7. We can now select our threshold and parameters for our custom alert
